And while your song is playing, Live Looper shows you exactly where you are within your track so you will never find yourself lost in your track again. The app supports the use of a USB footswitch for hands-free operation during live performance.  \r\n\r\nLive Looper plays pre-recorded backing track sound. You can either create backing track sound yourself using tools such as Band-In-A-Box, the Digitech Trio, Garage Band, LMMS, FL Studio (or similar), or by playing & recording live instruments; or you can use backing track sound created by others and available from many sources (the internet, etc.).\r\n\r\nVIDEO DEMOS:\r\nSearch for \"LiveLooperApp\" on YouTube.com to view video demos of the app in action.\r\n\r\nFEATURES:\r\n-Manage and play an unlimited number of full-song backing tracks with an unlimited number of parts (i.e. Intro, Verse, Chorus, etc.)\r\n-Specify the default play-sequence
